function SortByName(x,y) {
	return ((x.name == y.name) ? 0 : ((x.name > y.name) ? 1 : -1 ));
};
var MHAGSkills = Skills.slice(0,Skills.length-1);  // Copy Skills Array - do not include Torso Up!

function ShowPopup(ctype) {

	var l_popup = false; var l_separator = false;
	var o_popup = new PopupMenu();

	if ((ctype == "wpn") || (ctype == "tln")) {
		if (ctype == "tln") {
			if ($(ctype).value >= 72) {  // Auto-Guard!
			} else if ($(ctype).value >= 41) {  // Queen, King & Dragon -> Timeworn Charm
				o_popup.add('Timeworn Charm', function(target) { window.location='items.php?type='+ctype+'&id=408'; });
				l_popup = true;
				l_separator = true;
			} else if ($(ctype).value >= 18) { // Knight & Rook -> Shining Charm
				o_popup.add('Shining Charm', function(target) { window.location='items.php?type='+ctype+'&id=407'; });
				l_popup = true;
				l_separator = true;
			} else if ($(ctype).value >= 0) { // Pawn & Bishop -> Mystery Charm
				o_popup.add('Mystery Charm', function(target) { window.location='items.php?type='+ctype+'&id=406'; });
				l_popup = true;
				l_separator = true;
			};
		};
	} else if ($(ctype).value >= 0) {
		o_popup.add($(ctype).options[$(ctype).selectedIndex].text, function(target) { window.location='armors.php?type='+ctype+'&id='+$(ctype).value; });
		l_popup = true;
		l_separator = true;
	};
	if (!isHidden($(ctype+"slot1")) && !$(ctype+"slot1").disabled && $(ctype+"slot1").value >= 0) {
		if (l_separator) { o_popup.addSeparator(); l_separator = false; };
		o_popup.add($(ctype+"slot1").options[$(ctype+"slot1").selectedIndex].text, function(target) { window.location='armors.php?type=drn&id='+$(ctype+"slot1").value; });
		l_popup = true
	};
	if (!isHidden($(ctype+"slot2")) && !$(ctype+"slot2").disabled && $(ctype+"slot2").value > 0) {
		if (l_separator) { o_popup.addSeparator(); l_separator = false; };
		o_popup.add($(ctype+"slot2").options[$(ctype+"slot2").selectedIndex].text, function(target) { window.location='armors.php?type=drn&id='+$(ctype+"slot2").value; });
		l_popup = true
	};
	if (!isHidden($(ctype+"slot3")) && !$(ctype+"slot3").disabled && $(ctype+"slot3").value > 0) {
		if (l_separator) { o_popup.addSeparator(); l_separator = false; };
		o_popup.add($(ctype+"slot3").options[$(ctype+"slot3").selectedIndex].text, function(target) { window.location='armors.php?type=drn&id='+$(ctype+"slot3").value; });
		l_popup = true
	};
	if (!l_popup) o_popup.add('(none)', function(target) {} );
	o_popup.setSize(150, 0);
	o_popup.bind(ctype+'Info');
	o_popup.show();
};

</script>

<script type="text/javascript"><!--

function ShowSkillGroupHeader(c_GroupId,c_GroupDesc,n_BegRow,n_EndRow) {
	document.write('<INPUT ID="' + c_GroupId + '" TYPE=BUTTON VALUE=" - " onClick="' + "ShowHideRows('feox_skills_table'," + n_BegRow + "," + n_EndRow + ",'" + c_GroupId + "'" +')" STYLE="font-family: monospace; font-size: 11px;" /><B>' + c_GroupDesc + '</B>');
};

function ShowSkillDescription(c_Skill,n_Points) {
	var x = -1;
	for (var i=0;i<Skills.length;i++) {
		if (Skills[i]["name"] == c_Skill) { x = i; break; };
	};
	return ('<SPAN TITLE="'+getActivatedSkillDescription(Skills[x], n_Points)+'" STYLE="cursor:pointer">'+getActivatedSkill(Skills[x], n_Points)+'</SPAN> = '+c_Skill+' +'+n_Points);
};

function ShowHideRows(c_Table,n_Beg,n_End,c_Button) {
	var t = $(c_Table);
	for (var i=n_Beg;i<=n_End;i++) {
		t.rows[i].style.display = ((t.rows[i].style.display=="none")?"":"none");
	};
	$(c_Button).value = ((t.rows[n_Beg].style.display == "none") ? " + ":" - ");
	xsetCookie(c_Button,$(c_Button).value);
};

//--></script>
